insert into FIELDCOD_ZNMAT065temp1_70 SELECT DISTINCT FIELDCOD FROM ZNMAT065  ;
insert into ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp1_70 SELECT DISTINCT ORGANLEAF FROM ZNMAT046 join FIELDCOD_ZNMAT065temp1_70 on ZNMAT046.ORGANCOD = FIELDCOD_ZNMAT065temp1_70.FIELDCOD  ;
insert into DATYPE_ZNMAT088temp1_70 SELECT DISTINCT DATYPE FROM ZNMAT088 ;
insert into FIELDCOD_ZNMAT065temp2_70 SELECT DISTINCT FIELDCOD FROM ZNMAT065  ;
insert into ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp2_70 SELECT DISTINCT ORGANLEAF FROM ZNMAT046 join FIELDCOD_ZNMAT065temp2_70 on ZNMAT046.ORGANCOD = FIELDCOD_ZNMAT065temp2_70.FIELDCOD  ;
insert into FIELDCOD_ZNMAT065temp3_70  SELECT DISTINCT FIELDCOD FROM ZNMAT065  ;
insert into LINELEAF_ZNMAT024temp1_70 SELECT DISTINCT LINELEAF FROM ZNMAT024 join FIELDCOD_ZNMAT065temp3_70 on ZNMAT024.LINECOD = FIELDCOD_ZNMAT065temp3_70.FIELDCOD  ;
insert into LOB_COKEY_ZNMAT021temp1_70  SELECT DISTINCT LOB_COKEY FROM ZNMAT021 join LINELEAF_ZNMAT024temp1_70 on ZNMAT021.LOB_WD_VAL = LINELEAF_ZNMAT024temp1_70.LINELEAF  ;
insert into PRDLEAF_ZNMAT023temp1_70(PRDLEAF) SELECT DISTINCT PRDLEAF FROM ZNMAT023  ;
insert into PRD_COKEY_ZNMAT020temp1_70(PRD_COKEY)SELECT DISTINCT PRD_COKEY FROM ZNMAT020 join PRDLEAF_ZNMAT023temp1_70 on PRDLEAF_ZNMAT023temp1_70.PRDLEAF=ZNMAT020.PRD_WD_VAL   ;
insert into ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp3_70  SELECT DISTINCT ORGANLEAF FROM ZNMAT046  ;
insert into LINELEAF_ZNMAT024temp2_70 SELECT DISTINCT LINELEAF FROM ZNMAT024  ;
insert into LOB_COKEY_ZNMAT021temp2_70  SELECT DISTINCT LOB_COKEY FROM ZNMAT021 join LINELEAF_ZNMAT024temp2_70 on ZNMAT021.LOB_WD_VAL = LINELEAF_ZNMAT024temp2_70.LINELEAF  ;
insert into LINELEAF_ZNMAT024temp3_70 SELECT DISTINCT LINELEAF FROM ZNMAT024  ;
insert into LOB_COKEY_ZNMAT021temp3_70  SELECT LOB_COKEY FROM ZNMAT021 join LINELEAF_ZNMAT024temp3_70 on ZNMAT021.LOB_WD_VAL = LINELEAF_ZNMAT024temp3_70.LINELEAF  ;
insert into LINELEAF_ZNMAT024temp4_70 SELECT DISTINCT LINELEAF FROM ZNMAT024  ;
insert into LOB_COKEY_ZNMAT021temp4_70  SELECT DISTINCT LOB_COKEY FROM ZNMAT021 join LINELEAF_ZNMAT024temp4_70 on ZNMAT021.LOB_WD_VAL = LINELEAF_ZNMAT024temp4_70.LINELEAF  ;
